10.8535L2.46966 6.03032L1.93933 5.49999L2.99999 4.43933L3.53032 4.96966L7.99999 9.43933L12.4697 4.96966L13 4.43933L14.0607 5.49999Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg></button></div></div><time class="text-copy-14 text-gray-900 order-2 md:order-3" dateTime="2026-02-03">Feb 3, 2026</time></div><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">Agents fetch web pages to answer questions, write code, and complete tasks. When an agent requests a page, it gets everything your browser gets, including navigation menus, stylesheets, JavaScript bundles, tracking scripts, and footer links, when all it needs is the structured text on the page. That extra markup confuses the agent, consumes its context window, and makes every request more expensive.</p><h2 class="text-heading-24 md:text-heading-32 font-semibold pt-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:pt-6 [#changelog-description_&amp;:first-child]:pt-0 w-full group relative text-module__qZtYrq__subheading"><a class="flex items-center justify-center flex-col absolute left-0 bottom-0 mt-auto mb-auto w-8 h-8 rounded-full opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 -translate-x-3/4 group-hover:-translate-x-full delay-75 duration-300 transition-all text-gray-900 hover:text-gray-1000 hover:scale-110 focus-visible:-translate-x-full focus-visible:opacity-100 top-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:hidden" href="#what-is-content-negotiation" id="what-is-content-negotiation" style="scroll-margin-top:90px"><svg data-testid="geist-icon" height="16" stroke-linejoin="round" style="color:currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M8.46968 1.46968C10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 -0.203923 14.5303 1.46968C16.2039 3.14329 16.2039 5.85674 14.5303 7.53034L12.0303 10.0303L10.9697 8.96968L13.4697 6.46968C14.5575 5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 13.4697 2.53034C12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 1.44252 9.53034 2.53034L7.03034 5.03034L5.96968 3.96968L8.46968 1.46968ZM11.5303 5.53034L5.53034 11.5303L4.46968 10.4697L10.4697 4.46968L11.5303 5.53034ZM1.46968 14.5303C3.14329 16.2039 5.85673 16.204 7.53034 14.5303L10.0303 12.0303L8.96968 10.9697L6.46968 13.4697C5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 14.5575 2.53034 13.4697C1.44252 12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 2.53034 9.53034L5.03034 7.03034L3.96968 5.96968L1.46968 8.46968C-0.203923 10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 1.46968 14.5303Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg><span class="sr-only">Link to heading</span></a>What is content negotiation</h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">What agents need is a way to request just the text content of a page, without the browser-specific markup. <b>Content negotiation</b> solves this. It&#x27;s a standard HTTP mechanism where the client specifies its preferred format via the <code>Accept</code> header, and the server returns the matching representation. Many agents already send <code>Accept: text/markdown</code> when fetching pages, and a server that supports content negotiation can return clean, structured text from the same URL that serves HTML to a browser.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">We&#x27;ve updated many of our pages, including our blog and changelog, to support content negotiation. This post walks through how it works, how we implemented it in Next.js, and how to add markdown sitemaps so agents can discover your content.</p><h2 class="text-heading-24 md:text-heading-32 font-semibold pt-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:pt-6 [#changelog-description_&amp;:first-child]:pt-0 w-full group relative text-module__qZtYrq__subheading"><a class="flex items-center justify-center flex-col absolute left-0 bottom-0 mt-auto mb-auto w-8 h-8 rounded-full opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 -translate-x-3/4 group-hover:-translate-x-full delay-75 duration-300 transition-all text-gray-900 hover:text-gray-1000 hover:scale-110 focus-visible:-translate-x-full focus-visible:opacity-100 top-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:hidden" href="#how-agents-request-markdown" id="how-agents-request-markdown" style="scroll-margin-top:90px"><svg data-testid="geist-icon" height="16" stroke-linejoin="round" style="color:currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M8.46968 1.46968C10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 -0.203923 14.5303 1.46968C16.2039 3.14329 16.2039 5.85674 14.5303 7.53034L12.0303 10.0303L10.9697 8.96968L13.4697 6.46968C14.5575 5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 13.4697 2.53034C12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 1.44252 9.53034 2.53034L7.03034 5.03034L5.96968 3.96968L8.46968 1.46968ZM11.5303 5.53034L5.53034 11.5303L4.46968 10.4697L10.4697 4.46968L11.5303 5.53034ZM1.46968 14.5303C3.14329 16.2039 5.85673 16.204 7.53034 14.5303L10.0303 12.0303L8.96968 10.9697L6.46968 13.4697C5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 14.5575 2.53034 13.4697C1.44252 12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 2.53034 9.53034L5.03034 7.03034L3.96968 5.96968L1.46968 8.46968C-0.203923 10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 1.46968 14.5303Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg><span class="sr-only">Link to heading</span></a>How agents request markdown</h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">When an agent fetches a page, it includes an <code>Accept</code> header with its format preferences:</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph"><code>Accept: text/markdown, text/html, */*</code></p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">By listing <code>text/markdown</code> first, the agent signals that markdown is preferred over HTML when available. This works better than hosting separate <code>.md</code> URLs because content negotiation requires no site-specific knowledge. Any agent that sends the right header gets markdown automatically, from any site that supports it.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">Try it yourself:</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph"><code>curl https://vercel.com/blog/self-driving-infrastructure -H &quot;accept: text/markdown&quot;</code></p><h2 class="text-heading-24 md:text-heading-32 font-semibold pt-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:pt-6 [#changelog-description_&amp;:first-child]:pt-0 w-full group relative text-module__qZtYrq__subheading"><a class="flex items-center justify-center flex-col absolute left-0 bottom-0 mt-auto mb-auto w-8 h-8 rounded-full opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 -translate-x-3/4 group-hover:-translate-x-full delay-75 duration-300 transition-all text-gray-900 hover:text-gray-1000 hover:scale-110 focus-visible:-translate-x-full focus-visible:opacity-100 top-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:hidden" href="#implementing-content-negotiation-in-next.js" id="implementing-content-negotiation-in-next.js" style="scroll-margin-top:90px"><svg data-testid="geist-icon" height="16" stroke-linejoin="round" style="color:currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M8.46968 1.46968C10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 -0.203923 14.5303 1.46968C16.2039 3.14329 16.2039 5.85674 14.5303 7.53034L12.0303 10.0303L10.9697 8.96968L13.4697 6.46968C14.5575 5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 5.53034ZM1.46968 14.5303C3.14329 16.2039 5.85673 16.204 7.53034 14.5303L10.0303 12.0303L8.96968 10.9697L6.46968 13.4697C5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 14.5575 2.53034 13.4697C1.44252 12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 2.53034 9.53034L5.03034 7.03034L3.96968 5.96968L1.46968 8.46968C-0.203923 10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 1.46968 14.5303Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg><span class="sr-only">Link to heading</span></a>Implementing content negotiation in Next.js</h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">The implementation has two parts, a rewrite rule in <code>next.config.ts</code> that detects the header and a route handler that returns markdown.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">The rewrite checks the <code>Accept</code> header on every incoming request. When it contains <code>text/markdown</code>, the request gets routed to a dedicated markdown endpoint instead of the default HTML page:</p><div class="flex flex-col items-stretch justify-start gap-4 flex-initial blog-code-block-module__TEKDOa__wrapper"><div class="relative my-4 rounded-md border border-[var(--ds-gray-400)] overflow-hidden group/copy rounded-b-md bg-[var(--ds-bfackground-100)] Code blocks keep their syntax highlighting markers, headings maintain their hierarchy, and links remain functional. The agent receives the same information as the HTML version, just in a format optimized for token efficiency.</p><h2 class="text-heading-24 md:text-heading-32 font-semibold pt-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:pt-6 [#changelog-description_&amp;:first-child]:pt-0 w-full group relative text-module__qZtYrq__subheading"><a class="flex items-center justify-center flex-col absolute left-0 bottom-0 mt-auto mb-auto w-8 h-8 rounded-full opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 -translate-x-3/4 group-hover:-translate-x-full delay-75 duration-300 transition-all text-gray-900 hover:text-gray-1000 hover:scale-110 focus-visible:-translate-x-full focus-visible:opacity-100 top-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:hidden" href="#performance-benefits" id="performance-benefits" style="scroll-margin-top:90px"><svg data-testid="geist-icon" height="16" stroke-linejoin="round" style="color:currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M8.46968 1.46968C10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 -0.203923 14.5303 1.46968C16.2039 3.14329 16.2039 5.85674 14.5303 7.53034L12.0303 10.0303L10.9697 8.96968L13.4697 6.46968C14.5575 5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 13.4697 2.53034C12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 1.44252 9.53034 2.53034L7.03034 5.03034L5.96968 3.96968L8.46968 1.46968ZM11.5303 5.53034L5.53034 11.5303L4.46968 10.4697L10.4697 4.46968L11.5303 5.53034ZM1.46968 14.5303C3.14329 16.2039 5.85673 16.204 7.53034 14.5303L10.0303 12.0303L8.96968 10.9697L6.46968 13.4697C5.38186 14.5575 3.61816 14.5575 2.53034 13.4697C1.44252 12.3819 1.44252 10.6182 2.53034 9.53034L5.03034 7.03034L3.96968 5.96968L1.46968 8.46968C-0.203923 10.1433 -0.203925 12.8567 1.46968 14.5303Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg><span class="sr-only">Link to heading</span></a><b>Performance benefits</b></h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">The HTML version of this page is around 500KB. The markdown version is 3KB, a 99.37% reduction in payload size. For agents operating under token limits, smaller payloads mean they can consume more content per request and spend their budget on actual information instead of markup.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">We keep the HTML and markdown versions synchronized using <a href="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/api-reference/directives/use-cache-remote" rel="noopener" target="_blank" data-track="true" data-track-click-name="article_link" data-track-click-value="https://nextjs.org/docs/app/api-reference/directives/use-cache-remote" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline link-module__Q1NRQq__highlight [&amp;_u]:no-underline">Next.js 16 remote cache</a> and shared slugs, so when content updates in our CMS, both versions refresh simultaneously.</p><h2 class="text-heading-24 md:text-heading-32 font-semibold pt-[calc(var(--grid-divider-gap)/1.5)] in-[#changelog-description]:pt-6 [#changelog-description_&amp;:first-child]:pt-0 w-full group relative text-module__qZtYrq__subheading"><a class="flex items-center justify-center flex-col absolute left-0 bottom-0 mt-auto mb-auto w-8 class="sr-only">Link to heading</span></a>Markdown sitemaps for agent discovery</h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">Content negotiation also works for sitemaps. XML sitemaps are flat lists of URLs with no titles, no hierarchy, and no indication of what each page is about. A markdown sitemap gives agents a structured table of contents with human-readable titles and parent-child relationships, so they can understand what content exists on your site and navigate to what they need.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">We serve markdown sitemaps for both our blog and documentation.</p><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 agent-friendly</h2><p class="text-copy-16 lg:text-copy-18 text-module__qZtYrq__paragraph">Content negotiation, markdown sitemaps, and <code>link rel=&quot;alternate&quot;</code> tags give agents three ways to find and consume your content efficiently. You can read this page as markdown by sending <code>Accept: text/markdown</code> to any blog or changelog URL on vercel.com, as shown in the curl example above.</p><p class="text-copy-16
